## üîç Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### üéØ Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 73 page(s) - 120 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [landmark-unique](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-unique?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate
**Issue**: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<nav class="lb-header__nav lb-header-js-nav">
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
.lb-header__nav
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('.lb-header__nav')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://youtube.com/creators/search/
- https://youtube.com/trends/search/
- https://youtube.com/trends/articles/finding-your-inner-zen-on-youtube/
- https://youtube.com/intl/ar_ALL/creators/search/
- https://youtube.com/intl/cs_ALL/creators/search/
- *...and 68 more page(s)*

#### Pattern 2: Affects 63 page(s) - 63 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**Issue**: Target has insufficient size

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a class="lb-font-footnote" href="https://support.google.com/youtube/#topic=9257498">...</a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/a[@class="lb-font-footnote"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/a[@class="lb-font-footnote"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://youtube.com/

#### Rule: [SIA-R11: Button elements have an accessible name](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r11)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The link does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<a class="yt-simple-endpoint style-scope ytd-topbar-logo-renderer" id="logo" aria-label="" href="/">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@id="logo"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R12: Links have an accessible name](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r12)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The button does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<button id="button" class="style-scope yt-icon-button" aria-pressed="true">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@id="button"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<g id="chevron-left">...</g>`
- XPath: `/g[@id="chevron-left"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<g id="chevron-right">...</g>`
- XPath: `/g[@id="chevron-right"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<g id="arrow-drop-down">...</g>`
- XPath: `/g[@id="arrow-drop-down"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<g id="info">...</g>`
- XPath: `/g[@id="info"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<g id="menu">...</g>`
- XPath: `/g[@id="menu"]`

*... and 18 more failures for this rule*

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `navigation` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R64](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r64)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The heading does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<h1 class="ytdMiniplayerInfoBarTitle"></h1>`
- XPath: `/h1[@class="ytdMiniplayerInfoBarTitle"]`

- HTML: `<h1></h1>`
- XPath: `/h1`

- Message: There is no content between this heading and the next
- HTML: `<h1 class="ytdMiniplayerInfoBarTitle"></h1>`
- XPath: `/h1[@class="ytdMiniplayerInfoBarTitle"]`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The form field does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<input class="ytSearchboxComponentInput yt-searchbox-input title" name="search_query" aria-controls="i0" aria-expanded="true" type="text" autocomplete="off" autocorrect="off" spellcheck="false" aria-autocomplete="list" role="combobox" />`

- Message: Some `navigation` have the same name.

- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.18:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

- HTML: `<a class="lb-header__logo-wrapper lb-header-js-logo-wrapper" href="/intl/en_tw/creators/" aria-label="Homepage">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="lb-header__logo-wrapper lb-header-js-logo-wrapper"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="lb-font-footnote lb-font--no-crop                     lb-footer__minimal-link" href="https://www.youtube.com/t/terms">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="lb-font-footnote lb-font--no-crop                     lb-footer__minimal-link"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="lb-font-footnote" href="https://support.google.com/youtube/#topic=9257498">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="lb-font-footnote"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<select class="lb-font-footnote             lb-footer__language-select lb-js-footer-language-select" aria-label="Select language">...</select>`
- XPath: `/select[@class="lb-font-footnote             lb-footer__language-select lb-js-footer-language-select"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is not allowed for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R56: Landmarks with the same role are distinguishable](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r56)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `navigation` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R61](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r61)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The document does not start with a level 1 heading

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.18:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

- XPath: `/div[@id="copyright-match-tool"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element is either tabbable or has tabbable descendants
- HTML: `<div class="lb-tabpanel lb-tab-panel--initialized" lb-auto-init="LBTabpanel" lb-options="{                             'uid': 'copyright-protection-tools',                             'panelIndex': 'content-id'                           }" role="tabpanel" id="content-id" aria-labelledby="content-id" tabindex="-1" aria-hidden="true">...</div>`

- HTML: `<a href="https://blog.youtube/news-and-events/updates-youtube-supervised-accounts-teens/" target="_blank" aria-label="blog regarding custom reminder link opens in new tab" rel="noopener">customize</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is not allowed for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<button class="lb-tablist__tab lb-js-tablist-tab lb-font-weight-600 lb-tablist__tab--active" role="tab" value="children" id="children" tabindex="0" data-tabindex="-1" index="0" aria-selected="false">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@id="children"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<button class="lb-tablist__tab lb-js-tablist-tab lb-font-weight-600" role="tab" value="pre-teens" id="pre-teens" tabindex="0" data-tabindex="-1" index="1">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@id="pre-teens"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<button class="lb-tablist__tab lb-js-tablist-tab lb-font-weight-600" role="tab" value="teens" id="teens" tabindex="0" data-tabindex="-1" index="2">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@id="teens"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div class="lb-tabpanel lb-tabpanel--open lb-tab-panel--initialized" lb-auto-init="LBTabpanel" lb-options="{                     'uid': 'age-approporateness',                     'panelIndex': 'children'                   }" role="tabpanel" id="children" aria-labelledby="children" tabindex="0">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="children"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div class="lb-tabpanel lb-tab-panel--initialized" lb-auto-init="LBTabpanel" lb-options="{                     'uid': 'age-approporateness',                     'panelIndex': 'pre-teens'                   }" role="tabpanel" id="pre-teens" aria-labelledby="pre-teens" tabindex="-1" aria-hidden="true" data-tabindex="-1">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="pre-teens"]`

- XPath: `/button[@id="privacy-settings"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is not allowed for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div lb-auto-init="LBExpansionPanelTrigger" lb-expansion-panel-trigger-options="{'family': 'gollum', 'index': 0}" class="lb-expansion-panel__trigger lb-expansion-panel__trigger--reverse lb-expansion-panel-trigger--initialized lb-expansion-panel__trigger--hide" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="id-gollum-panel-1" id="id-gollum-panel-header-1">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="id-gollum-panel-header-1"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div class="lb-expansion-panel__surface" id="id-gollum-panel-1" role="region" aria-labelledby="id-lone-wolf-2-panel-header-1" style="--visibility--surface: hidden;" aria-hidden="true">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="id-gollum-panel-1"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<button class="lb-tablist__tab lb-js-tablist-tab lb-font-weight-600 lb-tablist__tab--active" role="tab" value="privacy-settings" id="privacy-settings" tabindex="0" data-tabindex="-1" index="0" aria-label="Privacy Settings" aria-selected="false">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@id="privacy-settings"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<button class="lb-tablist__tab lb-js-tablist-tab lb-font-weight-600" role="tab" value="ad-settings" id="ad-settings" tabindex="0" data-tabindex="-1" index="1" aria-label="Ad Settings">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@id="ad-settings"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div class="lb-tabpanel lb-tabpanel--open lb-tab-panel--initialized" lb-auto-init="LBTabpanel" lb-options="{                             'uid': 'privacy-tools',                             'panelIndex': 'privacy-settings'                           }" role="tabpanel" id="privacy-settings" aria-labelledby="privacy-settings" tabindex="0">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="privacy-settings"]`

- HTML: `<a class="lb-header__logo-wrapper lb-header-js-logo-wrapper" href="/intl/ALL_us/kids/">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="lb-header__logo-wrapper lb-header-js-logo-wrapper"]`

**Failure 2:**

- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="ytk-hero__description-subtitle lb-margin-bottom-xs">Your kids can</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ytk-hero__description-subtitle lb-margin-bottom-xs"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="ytk-hero__description-subtitle lb-margin-top-xs">on YouTube Kids</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ytk-hero__description-subtitle lb-margin-top-xs"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="lb-font-body ytk-peppa-pig__channel-subscriber">18.4M subscribers</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="lb-font-body ytk-peppa-pig__channel-subscriber"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="lb-font--no-crop">Peppa lives with her mummy and daddy and her littl...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="lb-font--no-crop"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit

- XPath: `/p[@class="ytk-peppa-pig__card-title lb-font-body lb-margin-top-xs lb-font--no-crop"]`

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://youtube.com/

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-attr](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-attr?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must only use supported ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<a id="endpoint" class="yt-simple-endpoint style-scope ytd-mini-guide-entry-renderer" aria-selected="true" aria-label="Home" title="Home" href="/">`
- XPath: `a[title="Home"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Elements must only use supported ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<a id="endpoint" class="yt-simple-endpoint style-scope ytd-mini-guide-entry-renderer" aria-selected="false" aria-label="Shorts" title="Shorts" href="/shorts/">`
- XPath: `a[title="Shorts"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Elements must only use supported ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<a id="endpoint" class="yt-simple-endpoint style-scope ytd-mini-guide-entry-renderer" aria-selected="false" aria-label="Subscriptions" title="Subscriptions" href="/feed/subscriptions">`
- XPath: `a[title="Subscriptions"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Elements must only use supported ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<a id="endpoint" class="yt-simple-endpoint style-scope ytd-mini-guide-entry-renderer" aria-selected="false" aria-label="You" title="You" href="/feed/you">`
- XPath: `a[title="You"]`
